---
title: Public API Changes in Aspose.Imaging 3.8.0
type: docs
weight: 90
url: /java/public-api-changes-in-aspose-imaging-3-8-0/
---

{{% alert color="primary" %}} 

This document describes the changes to the Aspose.Imaging API from version 3.7.0 to 3.8.0 that may be of interest to module/application developers. It includes new and updated public properties, methods, [added APIs](/imaging/java/public-api-changes-in-aspose-imaging-3-8-0-html/) and [removed classes etc.](/imaging/java/public-api-changes-in-aspose-imaging-3-8-0-html/) but also a description of any changes in the behavior behind the scenes in Aspose.Imaging.

{{% /alert %}} 
## **Added APIs**
